Cortana will send whatever you say after \"Control Home\" to your Premise server.  Your Premise server then uses a free SpeechParser module to translate the sentence into home automation commands that the Premise server performs.\r\n\r\nThis is done via a voice enabled Cortana service for hands free operation.  For hands-free operation just say \"Hey Cortana Control Home\" followed by a command phrase like \"turn on the master bedroom light.\"  Following a successful command, Cortana reads back exactly what your Premise server did, so you know for sure what task was performed.\r\n\r\nThe additional required software Premise Home Control and my Premise SpeechParser module are completely FREE, plus I show step by step videos on how to set everything up on my YouTube channel (see app support link).\r\n\r\nINSTALLATION:\r\nThis app requires that you have a working Premise Home Control server setup already, and it also requires that SpeechPraser be installed on the Premise server.
